Overview

=20

Bringing together the communities working in the environ= mental, animal and biomedical microbiome arenas, Microbiome is a for= um for presenting the very latest research and methodologies, as well as di= scussing current and future trends in microbiome research. With an expert i= nternational Editorial Board, Microbiome promotes collaboration and = foster common scientific objectives across a broad cross-section of sub-dis= ciplines within microbial ecology.
